<h1 _ngcontent-emk-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="hdc"> hdc </h1>

<div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>hdc（HarmonyOS Device Connector）是提供给开发人员的命令行调试工具，用于与设备进行交互调试、数据传输、日志查看以及应用安装等操作。该工具支持在Windows/Linux/MacOS系统上运行，为开发者提供高效，便捷的设备调试能力。</p>    <p>hdc包含三部分：</p>    <p><strong>客户端（client）</strong>：运行在电脑端的进程，开发者在执行hdc命令时启动该进程，命令结束后进程自动退出。</p>    <p><strong>服务器（server）</strong>：运行在电脑端的后台服务进程，用来管理客户端进程和设备端守护进程之间的数据交互，设备发现等。</p>    <p><strong>守护程序（daemon）</strong>：运行在调试设备端的进程，用来响应服务器发来的请求。</p>    <p>如图所示：</p>    <p><span><img originheight="159" originwidth="560" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115012.44383944619522928328726838203281:50001231000000:2800:5481B165B650825F7EEB500E230F3982686E6B1435F7A337AABD0CE9DDE816C0.png" width="560" height="159"></span></p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>客户端进程在启动时，默认会判断服务器进程是否正在运行。如果没有运行则会启动一个新的hdc进程作为服务器进程，运行在后台。</p>      <p>服务器运行时，默认会监听电脑端的8710端口。开发者可通过设置系统环境变量OHOS_HDC_SERVER_PORT自定义监听的端口号，范围为1~65535。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 332px;">     <h2 id="环境准备">环境准备<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="环境准备" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <p>hdc可以选择以下任意一种方式获取：</p>     <p>1.通过SDK获取hdc工具。SDK已嵌入<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/deveco-studio/" target="_blank">DevEco Studio</a>中，无需额外下载配置。hdc默认安装在DevEco Studio/sdk/default/openharmony/toolchains路径下，MacOS系统的sdk位于DevEco Studio/Contents目录下。</p>     <p>2.通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/download/" target="_blank">Command Line Tools</a>工具中的sdk目录获取相关工具。hdc程序默认安装在Command Line Tools/sdk/default/openharmony/toolchains路径下。</p>     <p>hdc支持USB和无线两种连接调试方式。在设备的设置&gt;系统&gt;开发者选项中开启或关闭调试开关 ，无需重启设备即可生效。如果设备未启用“开发者选项”，可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/ide-developer-mode#section530763213432" target="_blank">开发者选项</a>进行启用。具体调试连接方式及操作步骤请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#usb连接场景">USB连接场景</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#tcp连接场景">TCP连接场景</a>。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1412px;">     <h3 id="可选命令行直接执行hdc程序" class="firsth2">（可选）命令行直接执行hdc程序<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="可选命令行直接执行hdc程序" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><strong>安装目录下的调试</strong></p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>开发者可以在SDK的toolchains子目录下执行hdc命令进行设备调试。</p></li>      <li>       <p>hdc支持独立运行。将toolchains子目录下的hdc可执行文件和libusb_shared依赖文件集中存放至自定义目录中，在自定义目录下直接执行hdc命令，实现独立调试。</p></li>     </ul>     <p><strong>添加hdc到系统环境变量</strong></p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>Windows环境变量设置方法：</p>       <ol>        <li>按下Windows键，搜索栏输入“设置”，点击进入设置窗口；</li>        <li>在搜索栏中搜索“查看高级系统设置”。在环境变量&gt;系统变量&gt;Path&gt;编辑中，将hdc.exe所在目录添加到 Path。环境变量配置完成后，请重启电脑，即可在命令行窗口执行hdc命令。</li>       </ol></li>      <li>       <p>Linux/MacOS系统：</p>       <ol>        <li>         <p>打开终端工具，执行以下命令，根据输出结果分别执行不同的命令。</p>         <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>echo $SHELL</li></ol></pre></div></div>         <ol>          <li>           <p>如果输出结果为bin/bash，执行以下命令打开.bashrc文件。</p>           <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>vi ~/.zshrc</li></ol></pre></div></div></li>         </ol></li>        <li>         <p>切换至英文输入法，按下键盘字母“i”，进入Insert模式。</p></li>        <li>         <p>在文件末尾添加PATH信息。</p>         <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>export PATH={DevEco Studio}/sdk/default/openharmony/toolchains:$PATH</li></ol></pre></div></div>         <p>其中{DevEco Studio}需替换为DevEco Studio实际安装目录的绝对路径，例如/home/DevEco-Studio。</p></li>        <li>         <p>编辑完成后，单击Esc键退出编辑模式，输入“:wq”并且单击Enter键保存。</p></li>        <li>         <p>请执行以下命令，使配置的环境变量生效。</p>         <ol>          <li>           <p>如果步骤1打开的是.bashrc文件，请执行如下命令：</p>           <div    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 184px;">     <h3 id="可选服务器配置">（可选）服务器配置<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="可选服务器配置" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>配置系统环境变量可修改服务器进程的监听端口、日志打印级别或特性开关等。详细介绍请查看<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#可选配置项">可选配置项</a>章节。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>环境变量配置完成后，重启命令行窗口或其他使用到HarmonyOS SDK的软件，以生效新配置的环境变量。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 80px;">     <h2 id="hdc命令列表">hdc命令列表<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="hdc命令列表" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 720px;">     <h3 id="全局参数" class="firsth2">全局参数<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="全局参数" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>全局参数是指运行hdc命令时，可以添加在hdc和具体执行命令之间的参数。例如，使用-t参数可以选择指定的设备执行命令：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc -t connect-key shell echo "Hello world"</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.4.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.4.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#连接指定的目标设备">-t</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">通过设备标识符连接指定的目标设备。单台设备连接时为可选参数，连接多台设备时为必选参数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#服务器进程日志">-l</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定运行时日志等级，范围为数字0-6，默认为3（LOG_INFO）。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#远程连接场景">-s</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定客户端连接服务器时，服务进程的网络监听参数，格式为IP:port。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#快速执行命令">-p</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，绕过对服务进程的查询步骤，用于快速执行客户端命令。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#前台启动服务">-m</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，使用前台启动模式启动服务进程。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#创建正向端口转发任务">-e</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>可选参数，指定在TCP端口转发时，本地监听的IP地址，默认是127.0.0.1。该参数必须和-m一起使用。</p>          <p>使用-e参数指定监听地址时，如果监听地址不是本地回环地址（如127.0.0.1），需注意访问安全问题。</p>          <p><strong>说明</strong>：从API version 20开始，支持该接口。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1290px;">     <h3 id="命令列表">命令列表<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="命令列表" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div      <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#打开设备网络连接通道">tmode port</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#执行交互命令">shell</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">在设备端执行单次命令，例如hdc shell ls。无命令参数可进入设备端终端执行命令。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#安装应用文件">install</a></td>         <td href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#卸载应用">uninstall</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">卸载指定的应用包。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#本地发送文件至远端设备">file send</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106=""       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.4.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.4.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-h verbose</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">显示hdc命令帮助信息。可选参数：verbose，显示详细的帮助信息。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">help</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">显示hdc命令帮助信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.6.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.6.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>HarmonyOS device connector(HDC) ...</p>          <p>---------------------------------global commands:----------------------------------</p>          <p>-h/help [verbose] - Print hdc help, 'verbose' for more other cmds</p>          <p>...（此处省略详细帮助信息）</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">hdc命令使用帮助信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content">       <p>使用hdc时如出现异常，可尝试通过hdc kill -r命令终止异常进程并重启hdc服务。</p>       <p>如出现hdc list targets无法获取设备信息的情况，请参见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#设备无法识别">设备无法识别</a>章节。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 80px;">     <h2 id="设备连接管理">设备连接管理<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="设备连接管理" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 981px;">     <h3 id="查询设备列表" class="firsth2">查询设备列表<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="查询设备列表" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.4.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" width="50%">-v</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">显示设备更多详情。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.6.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.6.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设备标识符列表</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>已连接的设备标识符列表。</p>          <p>命令添加-v参数显示更多详情：设备标识符、连接方式（TCP/USB）、连接状态（Unknown/Ready/Connected/Offline/Unauthorized）、设备名称和hdc标识。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设备标识符 Unauthorized</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设备处于未授权状态。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Empty]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">没有查询到设备信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc list targets</span></li><li>connect-key1</li><li>...</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc list targets -v</span></li><li>connect-key1            USB     Connected       localhost       hdc</li><li>127.0.0.1:5555          TCP     Offline         localhost       hdc</li><li>connect-key2            USB     Offline         localhost       hdc</li><li>...</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1300px;">     <h3 id="连接指定的目标设备">连接指定的目标设备<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="连接指定的目标设备" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc -t [connect-key] [command]</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.4.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.4.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-t</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>通过设备标识符连接指定目标设备。</p>          <p>连接单台设备时为可选参数，连接多台设备时为必填参数。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">command</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">hdc支持的命令。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>connect-key为每个设备唯一的标识符。通过USB连接，标识符为设备序列号；通过网络无线连接设备，标识符格式为IP:port。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">正常执行返回信息，参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#命令列表">命令列表</a>具体说明。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]Not match target founded, check connect-key please.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">使用-t参数匹配不存在的connect-key，请检查connect-key是否正确。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]Device not founded or connected.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设备未找到或未连接。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]ExecuteCommand need connect-key? please confirm a device by help info.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">请确保已连接设备并打开调试开关。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">Unknown operation command...</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">不支持的命令。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>命令返回的错误信息仅供开发者参考，后续可能会优化调整。请勿将此类信息用于自动化脚本或程序的逻辑判断，实际程序交互建议使用系统异常提供的标准错误码，具体详情可参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#hdc错误码">hdc错误码</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <p>此调试方法需要与具体的操作命令搭配使用，下面以shell命令为例：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc list targets</span></li><li>connect-key1</li><li>...</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc -t connect-key1 shell <span class="hljs-built_in">echo</span> <span class="hljs-string">"hello world!"</span></span></li><li>hello world!</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 747px;">     <h3 id="等待设备正常连接">等待设备正常连接<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="等待设备正常连接" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc wait # 等待设备正常连接</li><li>hdc -t [connect-key] wait # 等待指定的设备正常连接，connect-key需要替换为指定的设备标识符</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.4.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.4.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-t connect-key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>3.1.0a版本新增参数：</p>          <p>连接单台设备时，为可选参数。</p>          <p>连接多台设备时，为必填参数。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.6.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.6.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">无</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">hdc wait命令执行后，识别到正常连接的设备后结束。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">如果设备正常连接，则命令执行结束无任何打印信息</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc <span class="hljs-built_in">wait</span> <span class="hljs-comment"># 单台设备</span></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc -t connect-key1 <span class="hljs-built_in">wait</span> <span class="hljs-comment"># 多设备需使用-t指定连接设备</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1028px;">     <h3 id="usb连接场景">USB连接场景<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="usb连接场景" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p><strong>环境确认</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.3.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">确认项</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.3.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">正常</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.3.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">异常处理</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">USB调试选项</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">开启。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">如果设备的USB调试模式未能自动开启，请尝试重启设备。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">USB数据连接线</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">使用USB数据连接线连接到调试电脑的USB接口。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">如果使用低带宽、无数据通信功能的USB连接线可能导致无法识别hdc设备，建议更换为设备原装充电线。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">USB接口</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">主板直出USB接口（台式机为后面板的USB接口，笔记本为机身的USB接口）。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">如果使用转接头/拓展坞/台式机前面板USB接口，可能存在带宽低和USB同步异常等问题，会导致频繁断连，推荐使用直连方式连接电脑和设备。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">hdc环境变量</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">终端命令行输入hdc -h有回显帮助信息内容。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">参见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#环境准备">环境准备</a>章节。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">驱动</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">连接hdc设备后，设备管理器通用串行总线设备存在设备“HDC Device”或“HDC Interface”。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">参见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#设备无法识别">设备无法识别</a>章节。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>连接步骤</strong></p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>通过USB连接设备。</p></li>      <li>       <p>执行以下命令查看已连接设备：</p>       <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc list targets</li></ol></pre></div></div>       <p>返回信息中包含设备标识符，表示USB连接成功。</p></li>      <li>       <p>查询到设备后，运行相关命令与设备交互。如果希望不带设备标识符执行hdc命令，需要确认设备不在TCP连接模式（hdc list targets查询的设备不包含IP:port形式的连接信息），直接连接即可，例如：</p>       <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc shell</li></ol></pre></div></div></li>     </ol>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 965px;">     <h3 id="tcp连接场景">TCP连接场景<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="tcp连接场景" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content">       <p>TCP调试功能尚未稳定，建议仅在测试环境中使用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>环境确认</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.4.1.1" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">确认项</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.4.1.2" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">正常</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.4.1.3" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">异常处理</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">网络连接</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">电脑、设备处于同一网络。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">连接同一WiFi。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">网络状态</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">telnet IP:port正常，网速稳定。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">请选择稳定网络。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">hdc环境变量</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">终端命令行输入hdc -h有回显帮助信息内容。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="33.33333333333333%">参见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#环境准备">环境准备</a>章节。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>连接步骤</strong></p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>在设备端设置&gt;系统&gt;开发者选项&gt;无线调试&gt;打开无线调试。</p></li>      <li>       <p>记录设备界面显示的IP地址和端口，格式为IP:port。</p></li>      <li>       <p>通过tcp连接设备，执行以下命令：</p>       <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc tconn IP:port</li></ol></pre></div></div>       <p>命令执行返回“Connect OK”表示连接成功。</p></li>      <li>       <p>查看已连接设备，执行以下命令：</p>       <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc list targets</li></ol></pre></div></div>       <p>返回信息为IP:port格式。</p>       <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">         <p>如果需要关闭TCP连接模式，可在设备中关闭无线调试开关或断开网络连接。</p>        </div></div></div></li>     </ol>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1869px;">     <h3 id="远程连接场景">远程连接场景<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="远程连接场景" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>远程连接场景指客户端（通常是开发者使用的本地电脑）通过网络与服务器（通常是连接了调试设备的服务器或开发机）建立连接，实现客户端对目标设备的远程调试，控制和管理。</p>     <p><span><img originheight="161" originwidth="608" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115012.59679522044177513797570070131935:50001231000000:2800:D9F6BDC501B97EE533C3374E5F1B01C2DB29954283D34F3A90FF22D14EB02540.png" width="608" height="161"></span></p>     <p>远程连接使用-s参数来指定服务器的网络参数，包括地址和端口号，该设置只在当前命令执行期间有效，命令格式如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc -s [IP:]port [command]</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.6.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">命令</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.6.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-s</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">指定当前服务进程的网络监听参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.8.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.8.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">IP</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定监听的IP地址，支持IPv4和IPv6。不指定IP默认监听本机127.0.0.1。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">port</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">指定监听的端口，范围为1~65535。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">command</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">hdc支持的命令，参见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#hdc命令列表">hdc命令列表</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.10.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.10.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">Connect server failed.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">与服务进程建立连接失败。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-s content port incorrect.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">端口号超出可设置范围（1~65535）。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">在已有服务进程，且服务进程的网络监听参数为127.0.0.1:8710的环境中，执行查询设备命令</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc -s 127.0.0.1:8710 list targets</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>连接步骤</strong></p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>服务器配置</p>       <p>服务器通过USB连接对应hdc设备后，执行以下命令：</p>       <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc <span class="hljs-built_in">kill</span>          <span class="hljs-comment"># 关闭本地hdc服务</span></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc -s IP:8710 -m <span class="hljs-comment"># 启动网络转发的hdc服务</span></span></li><li>                    # 其中IP为服务器自身的IP，windows可通过ipconfig查询，unix系统可通过ifconfig查询</li><li>                    # 8710是默认端口号，也可设置其他端口号如：18710</li><li>                    # 启动后服务器将打印日志</li></ol></pre></div></div></li>      <li>       <p>客户端连接</p>       <p>客户端可以连通服务器IP地址，满足条件后执行以下命令：</p>       <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc -s IP:8710 [<span class="hljs-built_in">command</span>] <span class="hljs-comment"># 其中IP为服务器IP，8710为第一步服务器进程启动时设置的端口号，</span></span></li><li>                           # 如果端口号有变化，这里也需要变更。</li><li>                           # command可以为任意hdc可用命令，例如list targets</li></ol></pre></div></div></li>     </ol>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当命令行中明确使用 -s 参数指定服务器进程端口时，系统将忽略OHOS_HDC_SERVER_PORT环境变量中定义的端口设置。使用 -s 参数指定服务器地址时，如果监听地址不是本地回环地址（如127.0.0.1），需注意访问安全问题。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 494px;">     <h3 id="usb调试和无线调试切换">USB调试和无线调试切换<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="usb调试和无线调试切换" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>用于连接模式切换的命令如下表所示：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.3.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">命令</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.3.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">tmode usb</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">该命令已废弃，不会操作设备连接通道，请在设备设置界面通过USB调试开关进行设置。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">tmode port [port-number]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">打开设备网络连接通道：设备端守护程序会重启，已建立的连接需要重新连接。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">tmode port close</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">关闭设备网络连接通道：设备端守护程序会重启，已建立的连接需要重新连接。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">tconn IP:port [-remove]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">连接指定设备，使用“IP:port”指定，使用-remove参数断开。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>推荐通过设备端的USB调试开关和无线调试开关来控制连接通道。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 992px;">     <h3 id="打开设备网络连接通道">打开设备网络连接通道<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="打开设备网络连接通道" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>命令格式如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc tmode port [port-number]</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.5.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.5.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">参数说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">port-number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">监听连接的网络端口号，范围：1~65535。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.7.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.7.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">Set device run mode successful.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设置成功。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]ExecuteCommand need connect-key.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">打开失败，设备列表为空，无法建立设备的无线调试通道。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]Incorrect port range.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">端口号超出可设置范围1~65535。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc tmode port 65512</span></li><li>Set device run mode successful.</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content">       <p>切换前，请确保条件满足：远端设备与近端电脑处于同一网络，可通过ping命令检查：</p>       <ol>        <li>         <p>近端电脑在命令行中执行命令ping 远端设备的IP地址；</p></li>        <li>         <p>如果能接收到远端设备的回应数据包，表明二者处于同一网络。</p></li>       </ol>       <p>如不满足以上条件，切勿使用该命令进行切换。</p>       <p>执行完毕后，远端守护程序将退出并重启，需要重新连接。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 599px;">     <h3 id="关闭网络连接通道">关闭网络连接通道<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="关闭网络连接通道" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>命令格式如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc tmode port close</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.5.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.5.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]ExecuteCommand need connect-key.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设备列表为空，无法执行命令。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc tmode port close</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>执行完毕后，远端设备上的守护程序将退出并重启，需要重新连接。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 870px;">     <h3 id="tcp连接设备">TCP连接设备<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="tcp连接设备" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>通过TCP连接指定设备，命令格式如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc tconn IP:port [-remove]</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.5.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.5.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">参数说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">IP:port</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设备的IP地址和端口号。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-remove</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，断开指定设备的连接。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.7.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.7.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">Connect OK.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">连接成功。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Info]Target is connected, repeat operation.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">设备当前已连接。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]Connect failed.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">连接失败。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc tconn 192.168.0.1:8888</span></li><li>Connect OK</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">断开指定网络设备连接</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc tconn 192.168.0.1:8888 -remove</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2350px;">     <h2 id="执行交互命令">执行交互命令<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="执行交互命令" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc shell [-b bundlename] [command]</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.4.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.4.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-b bundlename</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>3.1.0e版本新增参数。指定可调试应用包名，在可调试应用数据目录内，以非交互式模式执行命令。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/ide-device-file-explorer#section48216711204" target="_blank">命令行方式访问应用沙箱</a>。</p>          <p>此参数当前仅支持以非交互式模式执行命令，不支持缺省command参数执行命令进入交互式shell会话。</p>          <p>未配置此参数时，默认执行路径为系统根目录。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">command</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>需要在设备上执行的单次命令，不同类型或版本的系统支持的command命令有所差异，可以通过hdc shell ls /system/bin查阅支持的命令列表。当前大多数命令都是由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/toybox">toybox</a>提供，可通过 hdc shell toybox --help 获取命令帮助。</p>          <p>缺省该参数，hdc将会启动一个交互式的shell会话，开发者可以在命令提示符下输入命令，比如 ls、cd、pwd 等。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>使用参数[-b bundlename]指定包名，该包名对应的已安装应用必须满足以下条件：使用调试证书签名，并且已在设备上启动。有关如何申请调试证书及签名可参考：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/app/agc-help-add-debugcert-0000001914263178" target="_blank">申请调试证书</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">交互命令返回内容。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">返回内容详情请参见其他交互命令返回内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">/bin/sh: XXX : inaccessible or not found.</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">不支持的交互命令。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">[Fail]具体失败信息。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">执行失败，参见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hdc#hdc错误码">hdc错误码</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" <span class="hljs-string">"ps -ef | grep hdcd"</span></span></li><li>shell         39491      1 1 14:40:58 ?     00:00:00 hdcd</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 228px;">     <h2 id="应用管理">应用管理<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="应用管理" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.2.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">命令</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.2.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">install src</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">安装指定的应用文件。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">uninstall bundlename</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">卸载指定的应用package包名。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1955px;">     <h3 id="安装应用文件" class="firsth2">安装应用文件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="安装应用文件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>应用安装功能在设备端集成bm模块<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/bm-tool#安装命令install">安装命令（install）</a>，简化了安装流程，开发者可以在电脑端直接执行命令完成应用安装。命令格式如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc install [-cwd path|-r|-s|-w waitingTime|-u userId|-p|-h] src</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.5.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.5.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">src</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">应用安装包的文件路径。支持安装<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/hap-package">HAP</a>、应用内<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/in-app-hsp">HSP</a>。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-cwd</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>修改工作目录。</p>          <p>用于在应用安装时，切换src到指定path。例如，初始安装应用为test.hap，所在目录为C:\，实际安装应用文件路径为C:\test.hap；如果使用-cwd "D:\"，实际安装应用文件路径为D:\test.hap。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-r</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，覆盖安装一个HAP/HSP。默认缺省，缺省时表示覆盖安装。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-s</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">安装应用HSP时为必选参数，其他场景为可选参数。用于指定待安装应用间HSP的路径。指定目录的时候，每个路径目录下只能存在一个HSP。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-w</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，安装HAP时指定bm工具等待时间，最小的等待时长为180s，最大的等待时长为600s, 默认缺省为180s。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-u</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/bm-tool#userid">用户</a>，默认在当前活跃用户下安装应用。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-p</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定HAP路径，多HAP应用可指定多HAP所在文件夹路径。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-h</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，显示bm模块<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/bm-tool#安装命令install">安装命令（install）</a>帮助信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.7.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.7.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>[Info]App install path:XXX msg:install bundle successfully.</p>          <p>AppMod finish.</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">成功情况下返回安装信息及AppMod finish完成的通知。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">具体安装失败原因。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">失败情况下返回安装失败信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content">       <p>执行install命令使用bm模块命令参数，对-w和-u参数需参数值组合使用的情况，需将参数变量和参数值放在引号内使用，如"-w 180"，"-u 100"，防止参数解析异常导致命令执行失败。</p>      </div></div></div>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">安装example.hap包示例</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc install D:\example.hap</span></li><li>[Info]App install path:D:\example.hap msg:install bundle successfully.</li><li>AppMod finish</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">安装example.hap包示例（-r为bm模块install命令支持参数，覆盖安装）</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc install -r D:\example.hap</span></li><li>[Info]App install path:D:\example.hap msg:install bundle successfully.</li><li>AppMod finish</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">安装example.hsp包示例（-s为bm模块install命令支持参数，安装hsp必选参数）</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc install -s D:\example.hsp</span></li><li>[Info]App install path:D:\example.hsp msg:install bundle successfully.</li><li>AppMod finish</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">安装example.hap包示例（-w为bm模块install命令支持参数，指定bm工具等待时间）</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc <span class="hljs-string">"-w 180"</span> install D:\example.hap</span></li><li>[Info]App install path:D:\example.hap msg:install bundle successfully.</li><li>AppMod finish</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">安装example.hap包示例（-u为bm模块install命令支持参数，指定用户<span class="hljs-built_in">id</span>）</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc <span class="hljs-string">"-u 100"</span> install D:\example.hap</span></li><li>[Info]App install path:D:\example.hap msg:install bundle successfully.</li><li>AppMod finish</li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"></span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">安装D:\hap_dir下应用示例（-p为bm模块install命令支持参数，指定安装路径）</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_">$ </span><span class="language-bash">hdc -p install D:\hap_dir</span></li><li>[Info]App install path:D:\hap_dir msg:install bundle successfully.</li><li>AppMod finish</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1931px;">     <h3 id="卸载应用">卸载应用<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="卸载应用" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>应用卸载功能在设备端集成bm模块<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/bm-tool#卸载命令uninstall">卸载命令（uninstall）</a>，简化了卸载流程，开发者可以在电脑端直接执行命令完成应用卸载。命令格式如下：</p>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>hdc uninstall [-n|-m|-k|-s|-v|-u|-h] bundlename</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.5.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.5.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">bundlename</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">应用安装包。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-n</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定Bundle名称卸载应用。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-m</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，应用模块名称，指定卸载应用的一个模块。默认卸载所有模块。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-k</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，卸载应用时保存应用数据。默认卸载应用时不保存应用数据。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-s</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">根据场景判断，卸载应用间HSP时必选参数，其他场景为可选参数。卸载指定的共享库。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-v</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定共享包的版本号。默认卸载同包名的所有共享包。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-u</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，指定<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/bm-tool#userid">用户</a>，默认在当前活跃用户下卸载应用。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">-h</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">可选参数，bm模块<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/bm-tool#卸载命令uninstall">卸载命令（uninstall）</a>帮助信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回信息</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="layoutFixed idpTab">       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.3.1.1" valign="top" width="50%">返回信息</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.3.1.2" valign="top" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">          <p>[Info]App uninstall path: msg:uninstall bundle successfully.</p>          <p>AppMod finish.</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">成功情况下返回卸载信息和AppMod finish完成的通知。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">具体卸载失败原因。</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="50%">失败情况下返回卸载失败信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>使用方法</strong>：</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content">       <p>执行uninstall命令使用bm模块命令参数，对-m，-v和-u参数需参数值组合使用的情况，需将参数变量和参数值放在引号内使用，如"-m entry"，"-v 100001"和"-u 100"，防止参数解析异常导致命令执行失败。</p>      </div></div></div>     <div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-emk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="shell prettyprint linenums hljs language-shell" hw-language="shell" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-meta prompt_"># </span><span class="language-bash">卸载com.ohos.example包示例</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta
